function isElement(addedNode, selector, callback) {
if (
addedNode &&
typeof addedNode.querySelector === "function" &&

function getCookie(name) {
const match = document.cookie.match(
new RegExp("(^| )" + name + "=([^;]+)")
);
return match ? decodeURIComponent(match[2]) : null;
}

function setCookie(name, value, days) {
let expires = "";
if (days) {
let date = new Date();
date.setTime(date.getTime() + days * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000);

expires = "; expires=" + date.toUTCString();
}
document.cookie =
name +
"=" +
encodeURIComponent(value) +
expires +
"; path=/; SameSite=Lax; domain=.trendyol.com";
}

function handleRejected() {
OneTrust.RejectAll();
let optanonConsent = getCookie("OptanonConsent");

if (optanonConsent && !optanonConsent.includes("isRejected=true")) {
optanonConsent += "&isRejected=true";
setCookie("OptanonConsent", optanonConsent, 120);
}
}

function markConsentPending() {
var optanonConsent = getCookie("OptanonConsent");
if (!optanonConsent) return;

if (!optanonConsent.includes("isConsentPending=true")) {
optanonConsent = optanonConsent.replace(/&?isConsentPending=false/, "");
optanonConsent += "&isConsentPending=true";
setCookie("OptanonConsent", optanonConsent, 120);
}
}

function clearConsentPending() {
var optanonConsent = getCookie("OptanonConsent");
if (!optanonConsent || !optanonConsent.includes("isConsentPending=")) return;
optanonConsent = optanonConsent.replace(/&?isConsentPending=(true|false)/, "");
setCookie("OptanonConsent", optanonConsent, 120);
}

function navigateWithIgnore() {
var optanonConsent = getCookie("OptanonConsent");
if (!optanonConsent || !optanonConsent.includes("isConsentPending=true")) return;
optanonConsent = optanonConsent.replace("isConsentPending=true", "isConsentPending=false");
setCookie("OptanonConsent", optanonConsent, 120);
}

function handleNavigateClick(e) {
var target = e.target;
while (target && target !== document) {
if (target.tagName === "A" && target.href) {
navigateWithIgnore();
return;
}
target = target.parentElement;
}
}

for (
var j = 0, numNodes = mutations[i].addedNodes.length;
j < numNodes;
j++
) {

mutations[i].addedNodes[j],
"#onetrust-banner-sdk",
function () {
markConsentPending();
document.addEventListener("click", handleNavigateClick, true);
}
);
isElement(
mutations[i].addedNodes[j],
"#onetrust-reject-all-handler",
function () {
elementReadyObserver.disconnect();
document
.getElementById("onetrust-reject-all-handler")
.addEventListener("click", () => {
handleRejected();
});
}
);
}
}
});

window.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", () => {
elementReadyObserver.observe(document.body, {
attributes: false,
subtree: false,
childList: true,
});
});

function parseWithoutCategoryAbTests(type) {

if (type === "paymentAb") {
ab = "" !== "undefined" ? "" : "";
} else if (type === "fraudAb") {
ab = "" !== "undefined" ? "" : "";
}

.split("-")
.map((s) => s.trim())
.filter(Boolean);

return uniqueTests.map((test) => "AB" + test).join("-");
}
